     43          
     44          /*
     45           * Type of procedures which can be launched by the client.
     46           */
     47          enum procedure_type_t {
     48          	COMPLETE_DISCOVERY_PROCEDURE,
     49          	READ_PROCEDURE,
     50          	WRITE_PROCEDURE,
     51          	DESCRIPTOR_DISCOVERY_PROCEDURE
     52          };
     53          
     54          
     55          /*
     56           * Base class for a procedure control block
     57           */
     58          struct procedure_control_block_t {
     59          	/*
     60          	 * Base constructor for procedure control block.
     61          	 */
     62          	procedure_control_block_t(procedure_type_t type, Gap::Handle_t handle) :
     63          		type(type), connection_handle(handle), next(NULL) { }
     64          
     65          	virtual ~procedure_control_block_t() { }
     66          
     67          	/*
     68          	 * Entry point of the control block stack machine.
     69          	 */
     70          	virtual void handle(GenericGattClient* client, const AttServerMessage& message) = 0;
     71          
     72          	/*
     73          	 * Function call in case of timeout
     74          	 */
     75          	virtual void handle_timeout_error(GenericGattClient* client) = 0;
     76          
     77          	procedure_type_t type;
     78          	Gap::Handle_t connection_handle;
     79          	procedure_control_block_t* next;
     80          };
     81          
     82

    314          	UUID get_uuid(const AttReadByGroupTypeResponse::attribute_data_t& data) {
    315          		if (data.value.size() == 2) {
    316          			return UUID(data.value[0] | data.value[1] << 8);
    317          		} else {

    319          		}
    320          	}

    355          		static UUID get_uuid(const ArrayView<const uint8_t>& value) {
    356          			if (value.size() == 5) {
    357          				return UUID(value[3] | (value[4] << 8));
    358          			} else {
    359          				return UUID(value.data() + 3, UUID::LSB);
    360          			}
    361          		}
    362          
    363          		static DiscoveredCharacteristic::Properties_t get_properties(const ArrayView<const uint8_t>& value) {
    364          			uint8_t raw_properties = value[0];
    365          			DiscoveredCharacteristic::Properties_t result;
    366          			result._broadcast = (raw_properties & (1 << 0)) ? true : false;
    367          			result._read = (raw_properties & (1 << 1)) ? true : false;
    368          			result._writeWoResp = (raw_properties & (1 << 2))  ? true : false;
    369          			result._write = (raw_properties & (1 << 3))  ? true : false;
    370          			result._notify = (raw_properties & (1 << 4))  ? true : false;
    371          			result._indicate = (raw_properties & (1 << 5))  ? true : false;
    372          			result._authSignedWrite = (raw_properties & (1 << 6))  ? true : false;
    373          			return result;
    374          		}
    375          
    376          		static uint16_t get_value_handle(const ArrayView<const uint8_t>& value) {
    377          			return value[1] | (value[2] << 8);
    378          		}
    379          
    380          		void set_last_handle(uint16_t last_handle) {
    381          			lastHandle = last_handle;
    382          		}
    383          
    384          		bool is_valid() const {
    385          			return lastHandle != 0x0000;
    386          		}
    387          	};

    542          	void handle_error(GenericGattClient* client, const AttErrorResponse& error) {
    543          		ble_error_t status = BLE_ERROR_UNSPECIFIED;
    544          
    545          		switch (error.error_code) {
    546          			case AttErrorResponse::INVALID_HANDLE:
    547          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_PARAM;
    548          				break;
    549          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_AUTHORIZATION:
    550          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    551          				break;
    552          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_AUTHENTICATION:
    553          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    554          				break;
    555          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_SIZE:
    556          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    557          				break;
    558          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_ENCRYPTION:
    559          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    560          				break;
    561          			case AttErrorResponse::READ_NOT_PERMITTED:
    562          				status = BLE_ERROR_OPERATION_NOT_PERMITTED;
    563          				break;
    564          			case AttErrorResponse::INVALID_OFFSET:
    565          				status = BLE_ERROR_PARAM_OUT_OF_RANGE;
    566          				break;
    567          			case AttErrorResponse::ATTRIBUTE_NOT_LONG:
    568          				status = BLE_ERROR_PARAM_OUT_OF_RANGE;
    569          				break;
    570          			default:
    571          				status = BLE_ERROR_UNSPECIFIED;
    572          				break;
    573          		}
    574          

   \                                 In section .rodata, align 4, keep-with-next
    575          		GattReadCallbackParams response = {
   \                     ?_10:
   \   00000000   0x00000000         DC32 0
   \   00000004   0x0000 0x0000      DC16 0, 0, 0
   \              0x0000       
   \   0000000A   0x00 0x00          DC8 0, 0
   \   0000000C   0x00000000         DC32 0H
   \   00000010   0x00 0x00          DC8 0, 0, 0, 0
   \              0x00 0x00    
    576          			connection_handle,
    577          			attribute_handle,
    578          			offset,
    579          			error.error_code,
    580          			/* data */ NULL,
    581          			status
    582          		};
    583          
    584          		terminate(client, response);
    585          	}
    586          
    587          	uint16_t attribute_handle;
    588          	uint16_t offset;
    589          	uint16_t current_offset;
    590          	uint8_t* data;
    591          };

    731          	void handle_error(GenericGattClient* client, const AttErrorResponse& error) {
    732          		ble_error_t status = BLE_ERROR_UNSPECIFIED;
    733          
    734          		switch (error.error_code) {
    735          			case AttErrorResponse::INVALID_HANDLE:
    736          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_PARAM;
    737          				break;
    738          			case AttErrorResponse::INVALID_ATTRIBUTE_VALUE_LENGTH:
    739          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_PARAM;
    740          				break;
    741          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_AUTHORIZATION:
    742          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    743          				break;
    744          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_AUTHENTICATION:
    745          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    746          				break;
    747          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_SIZE:
    748          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    749          				break;
    750          			case AttErrorResponse::INSUFFICIENT_ENCRYPTION:
    751          				status = BLE_ERROR_INVALID_STATE;
    752          				break;
    753          			case AttErrorResponse::WRITE_NOT_PERMITTED:
    754          				status = BLE_ERROR_OPERATION_NOT_PERMITTED;
    755          				break;
    756          			default:
    757          				status = BLE_ERROR_UNSPECIFIED;
    758          				break;
    759          		}
    760          
    761          		if (error.request_opcode == AttributeOpcode(AttributeOpcode::PREPARE_WRITE_REQUEST)) {
    762          			clear_prepare_queue(client, status, error.error_code);
    763          		} else {

   \                                 In section .rodata, align 4, keep-with-next
    764          			GattWriteCallbackParams response = {
   \                     ?_16:
   \   00000000   0x00000000         DC32 0
   \   00000004   0x0000             DC16 0
   \   00000006   0x01 0x00          DC8 1, 0
   \   00000008   0x0000 0x0000      DC16 0, 0
   \   0000000C   0x00 0x00          DC8 0, 0, 0, 0
   \              0x00 0x00    
    765          				connection_handle,
    766          				attribute_handle,
    767          				GattWriteCallbackParams::OP_WRITE_REQ,
    768          				status,
    769          				error.error_code
    770          			};
    771          
    772          			terminate(client, response);
    773          		}
    774          	}

    837          	void handle_error(GenericGattClient* client, const AttErrorResponse& error) {
    838          		if (error.error_code == AttErrorResponse::ATTRIBUTE_NOT_FOUND) {

    873          	void terminate(GenericGattClient* client, ble_error_t status, uint8_t error_code = 0x00) {
    874          		client->remove_control_block(this);

    876          			characteristic,

    878          			error_code

    881          		delete this;
    882          	}
